create table company (company_name varchar(40), primary key (company_name));
create table brand_sales (brand_name varchar(15), date_year numeric(4,0), date_month numeric(2,0), gender char(1), income numeric(3,0), sales numeric(5,2), primary key (brand_name, date_year, date_month, gender, income) );
create table brand_info (brand_name varchar(15), dollar_amount_sold numeric(5,1), unit_sales numeric(5,2), company_name varchar(40), primary key (brand_name));
create table brand_model (brand_name varchar(15),model_name varchar(15), primary key (model_name));
create table model_info (model_name varchar(15), body_style varchar(15), month numeric(2,0), sales numeric(5,2), primary key (model_name, body_style, month));
create table vehicle(VIN varchar(15),model_name varchar(15),body_style varchar(15), brand_name varchar(15),color varchar(15), price numeric(5,2), primary key (VIN));
create table dealer (dealer_name varchar(15),keeping_average_time numeric(5,2), primary key (dealer_name));
create table customer(customer_name varchar(15),customer_phone varchar(15),dealer_name varchar(15),purchased_VIN varchar(15),customer_gender char(1),customer_income numeric(5,2),customer_indiv_com char(1),purchased_date DATE,primary key (customer_name, customer_phone, dealer_name, purchased_VIN));
create table plant_info(plant_name varchar(15),plant_role varchar(1),company_name varchar(40),primary key (plant_name));
create table supplier (supplier_name varchar(15), supplied_part varchar(15), primary key (supplier_name, supplied_part));
create table plant_supplier (plant_name varchar(15), supplier_name varchar(15), supplied_part varchar(15), supplied_date DATE, related_car_VIN varchar(15), primary key (plant_name, supplier_name, supplied_part, supplied_date, related_car_VIN) );
